		CREATE OptTemp TABLE create_as_target AS SelectStmt opt_with_data
				{
					/*
					 * When the SelectStmt is a set-operation tree, we must
					 * stuff the INTO information into the leftmost component
					 * Select, because that's where analyze.c will expect
					 * to find it.	Similarly, the output column names must
					 * be attached to that Select's target list.
					 */
					SelectStmt *n = findLeftmostSelect((SelectStmt *) $_[6]);
					if (n->intoClause != NULL)
						ereport(ERROR,
								(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),
								 errmsg("CREATE TABLE AS cannot specify INTO"),
								 parser_errposition(exprLocation((Node *) n->intoClause))));
					$_[4]->rel->relpersistence = $_[2];
					n->intoClause = $_[4];
					/* Implement WITH NO DATA by forcing top-level LIMIT 0 */
					if (!$_[7])
						((SelectStmt *) $_[6])->limitCount = makeIntConst(0, -1);
					return $_[6];
				}
		;

create_as_target:
			qualified_name OptCreateAs OptWith OnCommitOption OptTableSpace
				{
					return makeNode(IntoClause);
					$$->rel = $_[1];
					$$->colNames = $_[2];
					$$->options = $_[3];
					$$->onCommit = $_[4];
					$$->tableSpaceName = $_[5];
				}
		;

OptCreateAs:
			'(' CreateAsList ')'					{ return $_[2]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NIL; }
		;

CreateAsList:
			CreateAsElement							{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| CreateAsList ',' CreateAsElement		{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

CreateAsElement:
			ColId
				{
					ColumnDef *n = makeNode(ColumnDef);
					n->colname = $_[1];
					n->typeName = NULL;
					n->inhcount = 0;
					n->is_local = true;
					n->is_not_null = false;
					n->is_from_type = false;
					n->storage = 0;
					n->raw_default = NULL;
					n->cooked_default = NULL;
					n->collClause = NULL;
					n->collOid = InvalidOid;
					n->constraints = NIL;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

opt_with_data:
			WITH DATA_P								{ return TRUE; }
			| WITH NO DATA_P						{ return FALSE; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return TRUE; }
		;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERY :
 *				CREATE SEQUENCE seqname
 *				ALTER SEQUENCE seqname
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateSeqStmt:
			CREATE OptTemp SEQUENCE qualified_name OptSeqOptList
				{
					CreateSeqStmt *n = makeNode(CreateSeqStmt);
					$_[4]->relpersistence = $_[2];
					n->sequence = $_[4];
					n->options = $_[5];
					n->ownerId = InvalidOid;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

AlterSeqStmt:
			ALTER SEQUENCE qualified_name SeqOptList
				{
					AlterSeqStmt *n = makeNode(AlterSeqStmt);
					n->sequence = $_[3];
					n->options = $_[4];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

OptSeqOptList: SeqOptList							{ return $_[1]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NIL; }
		;

SeqOptList: SeqOptElem								{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| SeqOptList SeqOptElem					{ return lappend($_[1], $_[2]); }
		;

SeqOptElem: CACHE NumericOnly
				{
					return makeDefElem("cache", (Node *)$_[2]);
				}
			| CYCLE
				{
					return makeDefElem("cycle", (Node *)makeInteger(TRUE));
				}
			| NO CYCLE
				{
					return makeDefElem("cycle", (Node *)makeInteger(FALSE));
				}
			| INCREMENT opt_by NumericOnly
				{
					return makeDefElem("increment", (Node *)$_[3]);
				}
			| MAXVALUE NumericOnly
				{
					return makeDefElem("maxvalue", (Node *)$_[2]);
				}
			| MINVALUE NumericOnly
				{
					return makeDefElem("minvalue", (Node *)$_[2]);
				}
			| NO MAXVALUE
				{
					return makeDefElem("maxvalue", NULL);
				}
			| NO MINVALUE
				{
					return makeDefElem("minvalue", NULL);
				}
			| OWNED BY any_name
				{
					return makeDefElem("owned_by", (Node *)$_[3]);
				}
			| START opt_with NumericOnly
				{
					return makeDefElem("start", (Node *)$_[3]);
				}
			| RESTART
				{
					return makeDefElem("restart", NULL);
				}
			| RESTART opt_with NumericOnly
				{
					return makeDefElem("restart", (Node *)$_[3]);
				}
		;

opt_by:		BY				{}
			| /* empty */	{}
	  ;

NumericOnly:
			FCONST								{ return makeFloat($_[1]); }
			| '-' FCONST
				{
					return makeFloat($_[2]);
					doNegateFloat($$);
				}
			| SignedIconst						{ return makeInteger($_[1]); }
		;

NumericOnly_list:	NumericOnly						{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
				| NumericOnly_list ',' NumericOnly	{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERIES :
 *				CREATE [OR REPLACE] [TRUSTED] [PROCEDURAL] LANGUAGE ...
 *				DROP [PROCEDURAL] LANGUAGE ...
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreatePLangStmt:
			CREATE opt_or_replace opt_trusted opt_procedural LANGUAGE ColId_or_Sconst
			{
				CreatePLangStmt *n = makeNode(CreatePLangStmt);
				n->replace = $_[2];
				n->plname = $_[6];
				/* parameters are all to be supplied by system */
				n->plhandler = NIL;
				n->plinline = NIL;
				n->plvalidator = NIL;
				n->pltrusted = false;
				return (Node *)n;
			}
			| CREATE opt_or_replace opt_trusted opt_procedural LANGUAGE ColId_or_Sconst
			  HANDLER handler_name opt_inline_handler opt_validator
			{
				CreatePLangStmt *n = makeNode(CreatePLangStmt);
				n->replace = $_[2];
				n->plname = $_[6];
				n->plhandler = $_[8];
				n->plinline = $_[9];
				n->plvalidator = $_[1]0;
				n->pltrusted = $_[3];
				return (Node *)n;
			}
		;

opt_trusted:
			TRUSTED									{ return TRUE; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return FALSE; }
		;

/* This ought to be just func_name, but that causes reduce/reduce conflicts
 * (CREATE LANGUAGE is the only place where func_name isn't followed by '(').
 * Work around by using simple names, instead.
 */
handler_name:
			name						{ return list_make1(makeString($_[1])); }
			| name attrs				{ return lcons(makeString($_[1]), $_[2]); }
		;

opt_inline_handler:
			INLINE_P handler_name					{ return $_[2]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NIL; }
		;

validator_clause:
			VALIDATOR handler_name					{ return $_[2]; }
			| NO VALIDATOR							{ return NIL; }
		;

opt_validator:
			validator_clause						{ return $_[1]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NIL; }
		;

DropPLangStmt:
			DROP opt_procedural LANGUAGE ColId_or_Sconst opt_drop_behavior
				{
					DropPLangStmt *n = makeNode(DropPLangStmt);
					n->plname = $_[4];
					n->behavior = $_[5];
					n->missing_ok = false;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| DROP opt_procedural LANGUAGE IF_P EXISTS ColId_or_Sconst opt_drop_behavior
				{
					DropPLangStmt *n = makeNode(DropPLangStmt);
					n->plname = $_[6];
					n->behavior = $_[7];
					n->missing_ok = true;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

opt_procedural:
			PROCEDURAL								{}
			| /*EMPTY*/								{}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY:
 *             CREATE TABLESPACE tablespace LOCATION '/path/to/tablespace/'
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateTableSpaceStmt: CREATE TABLESPACE name OptTableSpaceOwner LOCATION Sconst
				{
					CreateTableSpaceStmt *n = makeNode(CreateTableSpaceStmt);
					n->tablespacename = $_[3];
					n->owner = $_[4];
					n->location = $_[6];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

OptTableSpaceOwner: OWNER name			{ return $_[2]; }
			| /*EMPTY */				{ return NULL; }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY :
 *				DROP TABLESPACE <tablespace>
 *
 *		No need for drop behaviour as we cannot implement dependencies for
 *		objects in other databases; we can only support RESTRICT.
 *
 ****************************************************************************/

DropTableSpaceStmt: DROP TABLESPACE name
				{
					DropTableSpaceStmt *n = makeNode(DropTableSpaceStmt);
					n->tablespacename = $_[3];
					n->missing_ok = false;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
				|  DROP TABLESPACE IF_P EXISTS name
                {
					DropTableSpaceStmt *n = makeNode(DropTableSpaceStmt);
					n->tablespacename = $_[5];
					n->missing_ok = true;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY:
 *             CREATE EXTENSION extension
 *             [ WITH ] [ SCHEMA schema ] [ VERSION version ] [ FROM oldversion ]
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateExtensionStmt: CREATE EXTENSION name opt_with create_extension_opt_list
				{
					CreateExtensionStmt *n = makeNode(CreateExtensionStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->if_not_exists = false;
					n->options = $_[5];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
				| CREATE EXTENSION IF_P NOT EXISTS name opt_with create_extension_opt_list
				{
					CreateExtensionStmt *n = makeNode(CreateExtensionStmt);
					n->extname = $_[6];
					n->if_not_exists = true;
					n->options = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

create_extension_opt_list:
			create_extension_opt_list create_extension_opt_item
				{ return lappend($_[1], $_[2]); }
			| /* EMPTY */
				{ return NIL; }
		;

create_extension_opt_item:
			SCHEMA name
				{
					return makeDefElem("schema", (Node *)makeString($_[2]));
				}
			| VERSION_P ColId_or_Sconst
				{
					return makeDefElem("new_version", (Node *)makeString($_[2]));
				}
			| FROM ColId_or_Sconst
				{
					return makeDefElem("old_version", (Node *)makeString($_[2]));
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * ALTER EXTENSION name UPDATE [ TO version ]
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

AlterExtensionStmt: ALTER EXTENSION name UPDATE alter_extension_opt_list
				{
					AlterExtensionStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->options = $_[5];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

alter_extension_opt_list:
			alter_extension_opt_list alter_extension_opt_item
				{ return lappend($_[1], $_[2]); }
			| /* EMPTY */
				{ return NIL; }
		;

alter_extension_opt_item:
			TO ColId_or_Sconst
				{
					return makeDefElem("new_version", (Node *)makeString($_[2]));
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * ALTER EXTENSION name ADD/DROP object-identifier
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

AlterExtensionContentsStmt:
			ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop AGGREGATE func_name aggr_args
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_AGGREGATE;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					n->objargs = $_[7];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop CAST '(' Typename AS Typename ')'
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_CAST;
					n->objname = list_make1($_[7]);
					n->objargs = list_make1($_[9]);
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop COLLATION any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_COLLATION;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop CONVERSION_P any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_CONVERSION;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop DOMAIN_P any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_DOMAIN;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop FUNCTION function_with_argtypes
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_FUNCTION;
					n->objname = $_[6]->funcname;
					n->objargs = $_[6]->funcargs;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop opt_procedural LANGUAGE name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_LANGUAGE;
					n->objname = list_make1(makeString($_[7]));
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop OPERATOR any_operator oper_argtypes
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_OPERATOR;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					n->objargs = $_[7];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop OPERATOR CLASS any_name USING access_method
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_OPCLASS;
					n->objname = $_[7];
					n->objargs = list_make1(makeString($_[9]));
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop OPERATOR FAMILY any_name USING access_method
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_OPFAMILY;
					n->objname = $_[7];
					n->objargs = list_make1(makeString($_[9]));
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop SCHEMA name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_SCHEMA;
					n->objname = list_make1(makeString($_[6]));
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop TABLE any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TABLE;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop TEXT_P SEARCH PARSER any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TSPARSER;
					n->objname = $_[8];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop TEXT_P SEARCH DICTIONARY any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TSDICTIONARY;
					n->objname = $_[8];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop TEXT_P SEARCH TEMPLATE any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TSTEMPLATE;
					n->objname = $_[8];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop TEXT_P SEARCH CONFIGURATION any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TSCONFIGURATION;
					n->objname = $_[8];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop SEQUENCE any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_SEQUENCE;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop VIEW any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_VIEW;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop FOREIGN TABLE any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_FOREIGN_TABLE;
					n->objname = $_[7];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop FOREIGN DATA_P WRAPPER name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_FDW;
					n->objname = list_make1(makeString($_[8]));
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop SERVER name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_FOREIGN_SERVER;
					n->objname = list_make1(makeString($_[6]));
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALTER EXTENSION name add_drop TYPE_P any_name
				{
					AlterExtensionContentsStmt *n = makeNode(AlterExtensionContentsStmt);
					n->extname = $_[3];
					n->action = $_[4];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TYPE;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY:
 *             CREATE FOREIGN DATA WRAPPER name options
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateFdwStmt: CREATE FOREIGN DATA_P WRAPPER name opt_fdw_options create_generic_options
				{
					CreateFdwStmt *n = makeNode(CreateFdwStmt);
					n->fdwname = $_[5];
					n->func_options = $_[6];
					n->options = $_[7];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

fdw_option:
			HANDLER handler_name				{ return makeDefElem("handler", (Node *)$_[2]); }
			| NO HANDLER						{ return makeDefElem("handler", NULL); }
			| VALIDATOR handler_name			{ return makeDefElem("validator", (Node *)$_[2]); }
			| NO VALIDATOR						{ return makeDefElem("validator", NULL); }
		;

fdw_options:
			fdw_option							{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| fdw_options fdw_option			{ return lappend($_[1], $_[2]); }
		;

opt_fdw_options:
			fdw_options							{ return $_[1]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/							{ return NIL; }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY :
 *				DROP FOREIGN DATA WRAPPER name
 *
 ****************************************************************************/

DropFdwStmt: DROP FOREIGN DATA_P WRAPPER name opt_drop_behavior
				{
					DropFdwStmt *n = makeNode(DropFdwStmt);
					n->fdwname = $_[5];
					n->missing_ok = false;
					n->behavior = $_[6];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
				|  DROP FOREIGN DATA_P WRAPPER IF_P EXISTS name opt_drop_behavior
                {
					DropFdwStmt *n = makeNode(DropFdwStmt);
					n->fdwname = $_[7];
					n->missing_ok = true;
					n->behavior = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY :
 *				ALTER FOREIGN DATA WRAPPER name options
 *
 ****************************************************************************/

AlterFdwStmt: ALTER FOREIGN DATA_P WRAPPER name opt_fdw_options alter_generic_options
				{
					AlterFdwStmt *n = makeNode(AlterFdwStmt);
					n->fdwname = $_[5];
					n->func_options = $_[6];
					n->options = $_[7];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| ALTER FOREIGN DATA_P WRAPPER name fdw_options
				{
					AlterFdwStmt *n = makeNode(AlterFdwStmt);
					n->fdwname = $_[5];
					n->func_options = $_[6];
					n->options = NIL;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

/* Options definition for CREATE FDW, SERVER and USER MAPPING */
create_generic_options:
			OPTIONS '(' generic_option_list ')'			{ return $_[3]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/									{ return NIL; }
		;

generic_option_list:
			generic_option_elem
				{
					return list_make1($_[1]);
				}
			| generic_option_list ',' generic_option_elem
				{
					return lappend($_[1], $_[3]);
				}
		;

/* Options definition for ALTER FDW, SERVER and USER MAPPING */
alter_generic_options:
			OPTIONS	'(' alter_generic_option_list ')'		{ return $_[3]; }
		;

alter_generic_option_list:
			alter_generic_option_elem
				{
					return list_make1($_[1]);
				}
			| alter_generic_option_list ',' alter_generic_option_elem
				{
					return lappend($_[1], $_[3]);
				}
		;

alter_generic_option_elem:
			generic_option_elem
				{
					return $_[1];
				}
			| SET generic_option_elem
				{
					return $_[2];
					$$->defaction = DEFELEM_SET;
				}
			| ADD_P generic_option_elem
				{
					return $_[2];
					$$->defaction = DEFELEM_ADD;
				}
			| DROP generic_option_name
				{
					return makeDefElemExtended(NULL, $_[2], NULL, DEFELEM_DROP);
				}
		;

generic_option_elem:
			generic_option_name generic_option_arg
				{
					return makeDefElem($_[1], $_[2]);
				}
		;

generic_option_name:
				ColLabel			{ return $_[1]; }
		;

/* We could use def_arg here, but the spec only requires string literals */
generic_option_arg:
				Sconst				{ return (Node *) makeString($_[1]); }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY:
 *             CREATE SERVER name [TYPE] [VERSION] [OPTIONS]
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateForeignServerStmt: CREATE SERVER name opt_type opt_foreign_server_version
						 FOREIGN DATA_P WRAPPER name create_generic_options
				{
					CreateForeignServerStmt *n = makeNode(CreateForeignServerStmt);
					n->servername = $_[3];
					n->servertype = $_[4];
					n->version = $_[5];
					n->fdwname = $_[9];
					n->options = $_[1]0;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

opt_type:
			TYPE_P Sconst			{ return $_[2]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/				{ return NULL; }
		;


foreign_server_version:
			VERSION_P Sconst		{ return $_[2]; }
		|	VERSION_P NULL_P		{ return NULL; }
		;

opt_foreign_server_version:
			foreign_server_version 	{ return $_[1]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/				{ return NULL; }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY :
 *				DROP SERVER name
 *
 ****************************************************************************/

DropForeignServerStmt: DROP SERVER name opt_drop_behavior
				{
					DropForeignServerStmt *n = makeNode(DropForeignServerStmt);
					n->servername = $_[3];
					n->missing_ok = false;
					n->behavior = $_[4];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
				|  DROP SERVER IF_P EXISTS name opt_drop_behavior
                {
					DropForeignServerStmt *n = makeNode(DropForeignServerStmt);
					n->servername = $_[5];
					n->missing_ok = true;
					n->behavior = $_[6];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY :
 *				ALTER SERVER name [VERSION] [OPTIONS]
 *
 ****************************************************************************/

AlterForeignServerStmt: ALTER SERVER name foreign_server_version alter_generic_options
				{
					AlterForeignServerStmt *n = makeNode(AlterForeignServerStmt);
					n->servername = $_[3];
					n->version = $_[4];
					n->options = $_[5];
					n->has_version = true;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| ALTER SERVER name foreign_server_version
				{
					AlterForeignServerStmt *n = makeNode(AlterForeignServerStmt);
					n->servername = $_[3];
					n->version = $_[4];
					n->has_version = true;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| ALTER SERVER name alter_generic_options
				{
					AlterForeignServerStmt *n = makeNode(AlterForeignServerStmt);
					n->servername = $_[3];
					n->options = $_[4];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY:
 *             CREATE FOREIGN TABLE relname (...) SERVER name (...)
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateForeignTableStmt:
		CREATE FOREIGN TABLE qualified_name
			OptForeignTableElementList
			SERVER name create_generic_options
				{
					CreateForeignTableStmt *n = makeNode(CreateForeignTableStmt);
					$_[4]->relpersistence = RELPERSISTENCE_PERMANENT;
					n->base.relation = $_[4];
					n->base.tableElts = $_[5];
					n->base.inhRelations = NIL;
					n->base.if_not_exists = false;
					/* FDW-specific data */
					n->servername = $_[7];
					n->options = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		| CREATE FOREIGN TABLE IF_P NOT EXISTS qualified_name
			OptForeignTableElementList
			SERVER name create_generic_options
				{
					CreateForeignTableStmt *n = makeNode(CreateForeignTableStmt);
					$_[7]->relpersistence = RELPERSISTENCE_PERMANENT;
					n->base.relation = $_[7];
					n->base.tableElts = $_[8];
					n->base.inhRelations = NIL;
					n->base.if_not_exists = true;
					/* FDW-specific data */
					n->servername = $_[1]0;
					n->options = $_[11];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

OptForeignTableElementList:
			'(' ForeignTableElementList ')'			{ return $_[2]; }
			| '(' ')'								{ return NIL; }
		;

ForeignTableElementList:
			ForeignTableElement
				{
					return list_make1($_[1]);
				}
			| ForeignTableElementList ',' ForeignTableElement
				{
					return lappend($_[1], $_[3]);
				}
		;

ForeignTableElement:
			columnDef					{ return $_[1]; }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY:
 *             ALTER FOREIGN TABLE relname [...]
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

AlterForeignTableStmt:
			ALTER FOREIGN TABLE relation_expr alter_table_cmds
				{
					AlterTableStmt *n = makeNode(AlterTableStmt);
					n->relation = $_[4];
					n->cmds = $_[5];
					n->relkind = OBJECT_FOREIGN_TABLE;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY:
 *             CREATE USER MAPPING FOR auth_ident SERVER name [OPTIONS]
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateUserMappingStmt: CREATE USER MAPPING FOR auth_ident SERVER name create_generic_options
				{
					CreateUserMappingStmt *n = makeNode(CreateUserMappingStmt);
					n->username = $_[5];
					n->servername = $_[7];
					n->options = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

/* User mapping authorization identifier */
auth_ident:
			CURRENT_USER 	{ return "current_user"; }
		|	USER			{ return "current_user"; }
		|	RoleId 			{ return (strcmp($_[1], "public") == 0) ? NULL : $_[1]; }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY :
 *				DROP USER MAPPING FOR auth_ident SERVER name
 *
 ****************************************************************************/

DropUserMappingStmt: DROP USER MAPPING FOR auth_ident SERVER name
				{
					DropUserMappingStmt *n = makeNode(DropUserMappingStmt);
					n->username = $_[5];
					n->servername = $_[7];
					n->missing_ok = false;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
				|  DROP USER MAPPING IF_P EXISTS FOR auth_ident SERVER name
                {
					DropUserMappingStmt *n = makeNode(DropUserMappingStmt);
					n->username = $_[7];
					n->servername = $_[9];
					n->missing_ok = true;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * 		QUERY :
 *				ALTER USER MAPPING FOR auth_ident SERVER name OPTIONS
 *
 ****************************************************************************/

AlterUserMappingStmt: ALTER USER MAPPING FOR auth_ident SERVER name alter_generic_options
				{
					AlterUserMappingStmt *n = makeNode(AlterUserMappingStmt);
					n->username = $_[5];
					n->servername = $_[7];
					n->options = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERIES :
 *				CREATE TRIGGER ...
 *				DROP TRIGGER ...
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateTrigStmt:
			CREATE TRIGGER name TriggerActionTime TriggerEvents ON
			qualified_name TriggerForSpec TriggerWhen
			EXECUTE PROCEDURE func_name '(' TriggerFuncArgs ')'
				{
					CreateTrigStmt *n = makeNode(CreateTrigStmt);
					n->trigname = $_[3];
					n->relation = $_[7];
					n->funcname = $_[12];
					n->args = $_[14];
					n->row = $_[8];
					n->timing = $_[4];
					n->events = intVal(linitial($_[5]));
					n->columns = (List *) lsecond($_[5]);
					n->whenClause = $_[9];
					n->isconstraint  = FALSE;
					n->deferrable	 = FALSE;
					n->initdeferred  = FALSE;
					n->constrrel = NULL;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE CONSTRAINT TRIGGER name AFTER TriggerEvents ON
			qualified_name OptConstrFromTable ConstraintAttributeSpec
			FOR EACH ROW TriggerWhen
			EXECUTE PROCEDURE func_name '(' TriggerFuncArgs ')'
				{
					CreateTrigStmt *n = makeNode(CreateTrigStmt);
					n->trigname = $_[4];
					n->relation = $_[8];
					n->funcname = $_[17];
					n->args = $_[19];
					n->row = TRUE;
					n->timing = TRIGGER_TYPE_AFTER;
					n->events = intVal(linitial($_[6]));
					n->columns = (List *) lsecond($_[6]);
					n->whenClause = $_[14];
					n->isconstraint  = TRUE;
					processCASbits($_[1]0, @10, "TRIGGER",
								   &n->deferrable, &n->initdeferred, NULL,
								   yyscanner);
					n->constrrel = $_[9];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

TriggerActionTime:
			BEFORE								{ return TRIGGER_TYPE_BEFORE; }
			| AFTER								{ return TRIGGER_TYPE_AFTER; }
			| INSTEAD OF						{ return TRIGGER_TYPE_INSTEAD; }
		;

TriggerEvents:
			TriggerOneEvent
				{ return $_[1]; }
			| TriggerEvents OR TriggerOneEvent
				{
					int		events1 = intVal(linitial($_[1]));
					int		events2 = intVal(linitial($_[3]));
					List   *columns1 = (List *) lsecond($_[1]);
					List   *columns2 = (List *) lsecond($_[3]);

					if (events1 & events2)
						parser_yyerror("duplicate trigger events specified");
					/*
					 * concat'ing the columns lists loses information about
					 * which columns went with which event, but so long as
					 * only UPDATE carries columns and we disallow multiple
					 * UPDATE items, it doesn't matter.  Command execution
					 * should just ignore the columns for non-UPDATE events.
					 */
					return list_make2(makeInteger(events1 | events2),
									list_concat(columns1, columns2));
				}
		;

TriggerOneEvent:
			INSERT
				{ return list_make2(makeInteger(TRIGGER_TYPE_INSERT), NIL); }
			| DELETE_P
				{ return list_make2(makeInteger(TRIGGER_TYPE_DELETE), NIL); }
			| UPDATE
				{ return list_make2(makeInteger(TRIGGER_TYPE_UPDATE), NIL); }
			| UPDATE OF columnList
				{ return list_make2(makeInteger(TRIGGER_TYPE_UPDATE), $_[3]); }
			| TRUNCATE
				{ return list_make2(makeInteger(TRIGGER_TYPE_TRUNCATE), NIL); }
		;

TriggerForSpec:
			FOR TriggerForOptEach TriggerForType
				{
					return $_[3];
				}
			| /* EMPTY */
				{
					/*
					 * If ROW/STATEMENT not specified, default to
					 * STATEMENT, per SQL
					 */
					return FALSE;
				}
		;

TriggerForOptEach:
			EACH									{}
			| /*EMPTY*/								{}
		;

TriggerForType:
			ROW										{ return TRUE; }
			| STATEMENT								{ return FALSE; }
		;

TriggerWhen:
			WHEN '(' a_expr ')'						{ return $_[3]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NULL; }
		;

TriggerFuncArgs:
			TriggerFuncArg							{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| TriggerFuncArgs ',' TriggerFuncArg	{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NIL; }
		;

TriggerFuncArg:
			Iconst
				{
					char buf[64];
					snprintf(buf, sizeof(buf), "%d", $_[1]);
					return makeString(pstrdup(buf));
				}
			| FCONST								{ return makeString($_[1]); }
			| Sconst								{ return makeString($_[1]); }
			| ColLabel								{ return makeString($_[1]); }
		;

OptConstrFromTable:
			FROM qualified_name						{ return $_[2]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NULL; }
		;

ConstraintAttributeSpec:
			/*EMPTY*/
				{ return 0; }
			| ConstraintAttributeSpec ConstraintAttributeElem
				{
					/*
					 * We must complain about conflicting options.
					 * We could, but choose not to, complain about redundant
					 * options (ie, where $_[2]'s bit is already set in $_[1]).
					 */
					int		newspec = $_[1] | $_[2];

					/* special message for this case */
					if ((newspec & (CAS_NOT_DEFERRABLE | CAS_INITIALLY_DEFERRED)) == (CAS_NOT_DEFERRABLE | CAS_INITIALLY_DEFERRED))
						ereport(ERROR,
								(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),
								 errmsg("constraint declared INITIALLY DEFERRED must be DEFERRABLE"),
								 parser_errposition(@2)));
					/* generic message for other conflicts */
					if ((newspec & (CAS_NOT_DEFERRABLE | CAS_DEFERRABLE)) == (CAS_NOT_DEFERRABLE | CAS_DEFERRABLE) ||
						(newspec & (CAS_INITIALLY_IMMEDIATE | CAS_INITIALLY_DEFERRED)) == (CAS_INITIALLY_IMMEDIATE | CAS_INITIALLY_DEFERRED))
						ereport(ERROR,
								(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),
								 errmsg("conflicting constraint properties"),
								 parser_errposition(@2)));
					return newspec;
				}
		;

ConstraintAttributeElem:
			NOT DEFERRABLE					{ return CAS_NOT_DEFERRABLE; }
			| DEFERRABLE					{ return CAS_DEFERRABLE; }
			| INITIALLY IMMEDIATE			{ return CAS_INITIALLY_IMMEDIATE; }
			| INITIALLY DEFERRED			{ return CAS_INITIALLY_DEFERRED; }
			| NOT VALID						{ return CAS_NOT_VALID; }
		;


DropTrigStmt:
			DROP TRIGGER name ON qualified_name opt_drop_behavior
				{
					DropPropertyStmt *n = makeNode(DropPropertyStmt);
					n->relation = $_[5];
					n->property = $_[3];
					n->behavior = $_[6];
					n->removeType = OBJECT_TRIGGER;
					n->missing_ok = false;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| DROP TRIGGER IF_P EXISTS name ON qualified_name opt_drop_behavior
				{
					DropPropertyStmt *n = makeNode(DropPropertyStmt);
					n->relation = $_[7];
					n->property = $_[5];
					n->behavior = $_[8];
					n->removeType = OBJECT_TRIGGER;
					n->missing_ok = true;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERIES :
 *				CREATE ASSERTION ...
 *				DROP ASSERTION ...
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateAssertStmt:
			CREATE ASSERTION name CHECK '(' a_expr ')'
			ConstraintAttributeSpec
				{
					CreateTrigStmt *n = makeNode(CreateTrigStmt);
					n->trigname = $_[3];
					n->args = list_make1($_[6]);
					n->isconstraint  = TRUE;
					processCASbits($_[8], @8, "ASSERTION",
								   &n->deferrable, &n->initdeferred, NULL,
								   yyscanner);

					ereport(ERROR,
							(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),
							 errmsg("CREATE ASSERTION is not yet implemented")));

					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

DropAssertStmt:
			DROP ASSERTION name opt_drop_behavior
				{
					DropPropertyStmt *n = makeNode(DropPropertyStmt);
					n->relation = NULL;
					n->property = $_[3];
					n->behavior = $_[4];
					n->removeType = OBJECT_TRIGGER; /* XXX */
					ereport(ERROR,
							(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),
							 errmsg("DROP ASSERTION is not yet implemented")));
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERY :
 *				define (aggregate,operator,type)
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

DefineStmt:
			CREATE AGGREGATE func_name aggr_args definition
				{
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_AGGREGATE;
					n->oldstyle = false;
					n->defnames = $_[3];
					n->args = $_[4];
					n->definition = $_[5];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE AGGREGATE func_name old_aggr_definition
				{
					/* old-style (pre-8.2) syntax for CREATE AGGREGATE */
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_AGGREGATE;
					n->oldstyle = true;
					n->defnames = $_[3];
					n->args = NIL;
					n->definition = $_[4];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE OPERATOR any_operator definition
				{
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_OPERATOR;
					n->oldstyle = false;
					n->defnames = $_[3];
					n->args = NIL;
					n->definition = $_[4];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE TYPE_P any_name definition
				{
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_TYPE;
					n->oldstyle = false;
					n->defnames = $_[3];
					n->args = NIL;
					n->definition = $_[4];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE TYPE_P any_name
				{
					/* Shell type (identified by lack of definition) */
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_TYPE;
					n->oldstyle = false;
					n->defnames = $_[3];
					n->args = NIL;
					n->definition = NIL;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE TYPE_P any_name AS '(' OptTableFuncElementList ')'
				{
					CompositeTypeStmt *n = makeNode(CompositeTypeStmt);

					/* can't use qualified_name, sigh */
					n->typevar = makeRangeVarFromAnyName($_[3], @3, yyscanner);
					n->coldeflist = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE TYPE_P any_name AS ENUM_P '(' opt_enum_val_list ')'
				{
					CreateEnumStmt *n = makeNode(CreateEnumStmt);
					n->typeName = $_[3];
					n->vals = $_[7];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE TEXT_P SEARCH PARSER any_name definition
				{
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_TSPARSER;
					n->args = NIL;
					n->defnames = $_[5];
					n->definition = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE TEXT_P SEARCH DICTIONARY any_name definition
				{
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_TSDICTIONARY;
					n->args = NIL;
					n->defnames = $_[5];
					n->definition = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE TEXT_P SEARCH TEMPLATE any_name definition
				{
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_TSTEMPLATE;
					n->args = NIL;
					n->defnames = $_[5];
					n->definition = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE TEXT_P SEARCH CONFIGURATION any_name definition
				{
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_TSCONFIGURATION;
					n->args = NIL;
					n->defnames = $_[5];
					n->definition = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE COLLATION any_name definition
				{
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_COLLATION;
					n->args = NIL;
					n->defnames = $_[3];
					n->definition = $_[4];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE COLLATION any_name FROM any_name
				{
					DefineStmt *n = makeNode(DefineStmt);
					n->kind = OBJECT_COLLATION;
					n->args = NIL;
					n->defnames = $_[3];
					n->definition = list_make1(makeDefElem("from", (Node *) $_[5]));
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

definition: '(' def_list ')'						{ return $_[2]; }
		;

def_list:  	def_elem								{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| def_list ',' def_elem					{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

def_elem:	ColLabel '=' def_arg
				{
					return makeDefElem($_[1], (Node *) $_[3]);
				}
			| ColLabel
				{
					return makeDefElem($_[1], NULL);
				}
		;

/* Note: any simple identifier will be returned as a type name! */
def_arg:	func_type						{ return (Node *)$_[1]; }
			| reserved_keyword				{ return (Node *)makeString(pstrdup($_[1])); }
			| qual_all_Op					{ return (Node *)$_[1]; }
			| NumericOnly					{ return (Node *)$_[1]; }
			| Sconst						{ return (Node *)makeString($_[1]); }
		;

aggr_args:	'(' type_list ')'						{ return $_[2]; }
			| '(' '*' ')'							{ return NIL; }
		;

old_aggr_definition: '(' old_aggr_list ')'			{ return $_[2]; }
		;

old_aggr_list: old_aggr_elem						{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| old_aggr_list ',' old_aggr_elem		{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

/*
 * Must use IDENT here to avoid reduce/reduce conflicts; fortunately none of
 * the item names needed in old aggregate definitions are likely to become
 * SQL keywords.
 */
old_aggr_elem:  IDENT '=' def_arg
				{
					return makeDefElem($_[1], (Node *)$_[3]);
				}
		;

opt_enum_val_list:
		enum_val_list							{ return $_[1]; }
		| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NIL; }
		;

enum_val_list:	Sconst
				{ return list_make1(makeString($_[1])); }
			| enum_val_list ',' Sconst
				{ return lappend($_[1], makeString($_[3])); }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *	ALTER TYPE enumtype ADD ...
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

AlterEnumStmt:
         ALTER TYPE_P any_name ADD_P VALUE_P Sconst
			 {
				 AlterEnumStmt *n = makeNode(AlterEnumStmt);
				 n->typeName = $_[3];
				 n->newVal = $_[6];
				 n->newValNeighbor = NULL;
				 n->newValIsAfter = true;
				 return (Node *) n;
			 }
		 | ALTER TYPE_P any_name ADD_P VALUE_P Sconst BEFORE Sconst
			 {
				 AlterEnumStmt *n = makeNode(AlterEnumStmt);
				 n->typeName = $_[3];
				 n->newVal = $_[6];
				 n->newValNeighbor = $_[8];
				 n->newValIsAfter = false;
				 return (Node *) n;
			 }
		 | ALTER TYPE_P any_name ADD_P VALUE_P Sconst AFTER Sconst
			 {
				 AlterEnumStmt *n = makeNode(AlterEnumStmt);
				 n->typeName = $_[3];
				 n->newVal = $_[6];
				 n->newValNeighbor = $_[8];
				 n->newValIsAfter = true;
				 return (Node *) n;
			 }
		 ;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERIES :
 *				CREATE OPERATOR CLASS ...
 *				CREATE OPERATOR FAMILY ...
 *				ALTER OPERATOR FAMILY ...
 *				DROP OPERATOR CLASS ...
 *				DROP OPERATOR FAMILY ...
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateOpClassStmt:
			CREATE OPERATOR CLASS any_name opt_default FOR TYPE_P Typename
			USING access_method opt_opfamily AS opclass_item_list
				{
					CreateOpClassStmt *n = makeNode(CreateOpClassStmt);
					n->opclassname = $_[4];
					n->isDefault = $_[5];
					n->datatype = $_[8];
					n->amname = $_[1]0;
					n->opfamilyname = $_[11];
					n->items = $_[13];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

opclass_item_list:
			opclass_item							{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| opclass_item_list ',' opclass_item	{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

opclass_item:
			OPERATOR Iconst any_operator opclass_purpose opt_recheck
				{
					CreateOpClassItem *n = makeNode(CreateOpClassItem);
					n->itemtype = OPCLASS_ITEM_OPERATOR;
					n->name = $_[3];
					n->args = NIL;
					n->number = $_[2];
					n->order_family = $_[4];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| OPERATOR Iconst any_operator oper_argtypes opclass_purpose
			  opt_recheck
				{
					CreateOpClassItem *n = makeNode(CreateOpClassItem);
					n->itemtype = OPCLASS_ITEM_OPERATOR;
					n->name = $_[3];
					n->args = $_[4];
					n->number = $_[2];
					n->order_family = $_[5];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| FUNCTION Iconst func_name func_args
				{
					CreateOpClassItem *n = makeNode(CreateOpClassItem);
					n->itemtype = OPCLASS_ITEM_FUNCTION;
					n->name = $_[3];
					n->args = extractArgTypes($_[4]);
					n->number = $_[2];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| FUNCTION Iconst '(' type_list ')' func_name func_args
				{
					CreateOpClassItem *n = makeNode(CreateOpClassItem);
					n->itemtype = OPCLASS_ITEM_FUNCTION;
					n->name = $_[6];
					n->args = extractArgTypes($_[7]);
					n->number = $_[2];
					n->class_args = $_[4];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| STORAGE Typename
				{
					CreateOpClassItem *n = makeNode(CreateOpClassItem);
					n->itemtype = OPCLASS_ITEM_STORAGETYPE;
					n->storedtype = $_[2];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

opt_default:	DEFAULT						{ return TRUE; }
			| /*EMPTY*/						{ return FALSE; }
		;

opt_opfamily:	FAMILY any_name				{ return $_[2]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/						{ return NIL; }
		;

opclass_purpose: FOR SEARCH					{ return NIL; }
			| FOR ORDER BY any_name			{ return $_[4]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/						{ return NIL; }
		;

opt_recheck:	RECHECK
				{
					/*
					 * RECHECK no longer does anything in opclass definitions,
					 * but we still accept it to ease porting of old database
					 * dumps.
					 */
					ereport(NOTICE,
							(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),
							 errmsg("RECHECK is no longer required"),
							 errhint("Update your data type."),
							 parser_errposition(@1)));
					return TRUE;
				}
			| /*EMPTY*/						{ return FALSE; }
		;


CreateOpFamilyStmt:
			CREATE OPERATOR FAMILY any_name USING access_method
				{
					CreateOpFamilyStmt *n = makeNode(CreateOpFamilyStmt);
					n->opfamilyname = $_[4];
					n->amname = $_[6];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

AlterOpFamilyStmt:
			ALTER OPERATOR FAMILY any_name USING access_method ADD_P opclass_item_list
				{
					AlterOpFamilyStmt *n = makeNode(AlterOpFamilyStmt);
					n->opfamilyname = $_[4];
					n->amname = $_[6];
					n->isDrop = false;
					n->items = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| ALTER OPERATOR FAMILY any_name USING access_method DROP opclass_drop_list
				{
					AlterOpFamilyStmt *n = makeNode(AlterOpFamilyStmt);
					n->opfamilyname = $_[4];
					n->amname = $_[6];
					n->isDrop = true;
					n->items = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

opclass_drop_list:
			opclass_drop							{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| opclass_drop_list ',' opclass_drop	{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

opclass_drop:
			OPERATOR Iconst '(' type_list ')'
				{
					CreateOpClassItem *n = makeNode(CreateOpClassItem);
					n->itemtype = OPCLASS_ITEM_OPERATOR;
					n->number = $_[2];
					n->args = $_[4];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| FUNCTION Iconst '(' type_list ')'
				{
					CreateOpClassItem *n = makeNode(CreateOpClassItem);
					n->itemtype = OPCLASS_ITEM_FUNCTION;
					n->number = $_[2];
					n->args = $_[4];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;


DropOpClassStmt:
			DROP OPERATOR CLASS any_name USING access_method opt_drop_behavior
				{
					RemoveOpClassStmt *n = makeNode(RemoveOpClassStmt);
					n->opclassname = $_[4];
					n->amname = $_[6];
					n->behavior = $_[7];
					n->missing_ok = false;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| DROP OPERATOR CLASS IF_P EXISTS any_name USING access_method opt_drop_behavior
				{
					RemoveOpClassStmt *n = makeNode(RemoveOpClassStmt);
					n->opclassname = $_[6];
					n->amname = $_[8];
					n->behavior = $_[9];
					n->missing_ok = true;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

DropOpFamilyStmt:
			DROP OPERATOR FAMILY any_name USING access_method opt_drop_behavior
				{
					RemoveOpFamilyStmt *n = makeNode(RemoveOpFamilyStmt);
					n->opfamilyname = $_[4];
					n->amname = $_[6];
					n->behavior = $_[7];
					n->missing_ok = false;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| DROP OPERATOR FAMILY IF_P EXISTS any_name USING access_method opt_drop_behavior
				{
					RemoveOpFamilyStmt *n = makeNode(RemoveOpFamilyStmt);
					n->opfamilyname = $_[6];
					n->amname = $_[8];
					n->behavior = $_[9];
					n->missing_ok = true;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERY:
 *
 *		DROP OWNED BY username [, username ...] [ RESTRICT | CASCADE ]
 *		REASSIGN OWNED BY username [, username ...] TO username
 *
 *****************************************************************************/
DropOwnedStmt:
			DROP OWNED BY name_list opt_drop_behavior
			 	{
					DropOwnedStmt *n = makeNode(DropOwnedStmt);
					n->roles = $_[4];
					n->behavior = $_[5];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

ReassignOwnedStmt:
			REASSIGN OWNED BY name_list TO name
				{
					ReassignOwnedStmt *n = makeNode(ReassignOwnedStmt);
					n->roles = $_[4];
					n->newrole = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERY:
 *
 *		DROP itemtype [ IF EXISTS ] itemname [, itemname ...]
 *           [ RESTRICT | CASCADE ]
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

DropStmt:	DROP drop_type IF_P EXISTS any_name_list opt_drop_behavior
				{
					DropStmt *n = makeNode(DropStmt);
					n->removeType = $_[2];
					n->missing_ok = TRUE;
					n->objects = $_[5];
					n->behavior = $_[6];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| DROP drop_type any_name_list opt_drop_behavior
				{
					DropStmt *n = makeNode(DropStmt);
					n->removeType = $_[2];
					n->missing_ok = FALSE;
					n->objects = $_[3];
					n->behavior = $_[4];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;


drop_type:	TABLE									{ return OBJECT_TABLE; }
			| SEQUENCE								{ return OBJECT_SEQUENCE; }
			| VIEW									{ return OBJECT_VIEW; }
			| INDEX									{ return OBJECT_INDEX; }
			| FOREIGN TABLE							{ return OBJECT_FOREIGN_TABLE; }
			| TYPE_P								{ return OBJECT_TYPE; }
			| DOMAIN_P								{ return OBJECT_DOMAIN; }
			| COLLATION								{ return OBJECT_COLLATION; }
			| CONVERSION_P							{ return OBJECT_CONVERSION; }
			| SCHEMA								{ return OBJECT_SCHEMA; }
			| EXTENSION								{ return OBJECT_EXTENSION; }
			| TEXT_P SEARCH PARSER					{ return OBJECT_TSPARSER; }
			| TEXT_P SEARCH DICTIONARY				{ return OBJECT_TSDICTIONARY; }
			| TEXT_P SEARCH TEMPLATE				{ return OBJECT_TSTEMPLATE; }
			| TEXT_P SEARCH CONFIGURATION			{ return OBJECT_TSCONFIGURATION; }
		;

any_name_list:
			any_name								{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| any_name_list ',' any_name			{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

any_name:	ColId						{ return list_make1(makeString($_[1])); }
			| ColId attrs				{ return lcons(makeString($_[1]), $_[2]); }
		;

attrs:		'.' attr_name
					{ return list_make1(makeString($_[2])); }
			| attrs '.' attr_name
					{ return lappend($_[1], makeString($_[3])); }
		;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERY:
 *				truncate table relname1, relname2, ...
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

TruncateStmt:
			TRUNCATE opt_table relation_expr_list opt_restart_seqs opt_drop_behavior
				{
					TruncateStmt *n = makeNode(TruncateStmt);
					n->relations = $_[3];
					n->restart_seqs = $_[4];
					n->behavior = $_[5];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

opt_restart_seqs:
			CONTINUE_P IDENTITY_P		{ return false; }
			| RESTART IDENTITY_P		{ return true; }
			| /* EMPTY */				{ return false; }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *	The COMMENT ON statement can take different forms based upon the type of
 *	the object associated with the comment. The form of the statement is:
 *
 *	COMMENT ON [ [ DATABASE | DOMAIN | INDEX | SEQUENCE | TABLE | TYPE | VIEW |
 *				   COLLATION | CONVERSION | LANGUAGE | OPERATOR CLASS |
 *				   LARGE OBJECT | CAST | COLUMN | SCHEMA | TABLESPACE |
 *				   EXTENSION | ROLE | TEXT SEARCH PARSER |
 *				   TEXT SEARCH DICTIONARY | TEXT SEARCH TEMPLATE |
 *				   TEXT SEARCH CONFIGURATION | FOREIGN TABLE |
 *				   FOREIGN DATA WRAPPER | SERVER ] <objname> |
 *				 AGGREGATE <aggname> (arg1, ...) |
 *				 FUNCTION <funcname> (arg1, arg2, ...) |
 *				 OPERATOR <op> (leftoperand_typ, rightoperand_typ) |
 *				 TRIGGER <triggername> ON <relname> |
 *				 CONSTRAINT <constraintname> ON <relname> |
 *				 RULE <rulename> ON <relname> ]
 *			   IS 'text'
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CommentStmt:
			COMMENT ON comment_type any_name IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = $_[3];
					n->objname = $_[4];
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->comment = $_[6];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON AGGREGATE func_name aggr_args IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_AGGREGATE;
					n->objname = $_[4];
					n->objargs = $_[5];
					n->comment = $_[7];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON FUNCTION func_name func_args IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_FUNCTION;
					n->objname = $_[4];
					n->objargs = extractArgTypes($_[5]);
					n->comment = $_[7];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON OPERATOR any_operator oper_argtypes IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_OPERATOR;
					n->objname = $_[4];
					n->objargs = $_[5];
					n->comment = $_[7];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON CONSTRAINT name ON any_name IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_CONSTRAINT;
					n->objname = lappend($_[6], makeString($_[4]));
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->comment = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON RULE name ON any_name IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_RULE;
					n->objname = lappend($_[6], makeString($_[4]));
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->comment = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON RULE name IS comment_text
				{
					/* Obsolete syntax supported for awhile for compatibility */
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_RULE;
					n->objname = list_make1(makeString($_[4]));
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->comment = $_[6];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON TRIGGER name ON any_name IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TRIGGER;
					n->objname = lappend($_[6], makeString($_[4]));
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->comment = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON OPERATOR CLASS any_name USING access_method IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_OPCLASS;
					n->objname = $_[5];
					n->objargs = list_make1(makeString($_[7]));
					n->comment = $_[9];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON OPERATOR FAMILY any_name USING access_method IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_OPFAMILY;
					n->objname = $_[5];
					n->objargs = list_make1(makeString($_[7]));
					n->comment = $_[9];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON LARGE_P OBJECT_P NumericOnly IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_LARGEOBJECT;
					n->objname = list_make1($_[5]);
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->comment = $_[7];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON CAST '(' Typename AS Typename ')' IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_CAST;
					n->objname = list_make1($_[5]);
					n->objargs = list_make1($_[7]);
					n->comment = $_[1]0;
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON opt_procedural LANGUAGE any_name IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_LANGUAGE;
					n->objname = $_[5];
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->comment = $_[7];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON TEXT_P SEARCH PARSER any_name IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TSPARSER;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					n->comment = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON TEXT_P SEARCH DICTIONARY any_name IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TSDICTIONARY;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					n->comment = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON TEXT_P SEARCH TEMPLATE any_name IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TSTEMPLATE;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					n->comment = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| COMMENT ON TEXT_P SEARCH CONFIGURATION any_name IS comment_text
				{
					CommentStmt *n = makeNode(CommentStmt);
					n->objtype = OBJECT_TSCONFIGURATION;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					n->comment = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

comment_type:
			COLUMN								{ return OBJECT_COLUMN; }
			| DATABASE							{ return OBJECT_DATABASE; }
			| SCHEMA							{ return OBJECT_SCHEMA; }
			| INDEX								{ return OBJECT_INDEX; }
			| SEQUENCE							{ return OBJECT_SEQUENCE; }
			| TABLE								{ return OBJECT_TABLE; }
			| DOMAIN_P							{ return OBJECT_DOMAIN; }
			| TYPE_P							{ return OBJECT_TYPE; }
			| VIEW								{ return OBJECT_VIEW; }
			| COLLATION							{ return OBJECT_COLLATION; }
			| CONVERSION_P						{ return OBJECT_CONVERSION; }
			| TABLESPACE						{ return OBJECT_TABLESPACE; }
			| EXTENSION 						{ return OBJECT_EXTENSION; }
			| ROLE								{ return OBJECT_ROLE; }
			| FOREIGN TABLE						{ return OBJECT_FOREIGN_TABLE; }
			| SERVER							{ return OBJECT_FOREIGN_SERVER; }
			| FOREIGN DATA_P WRAPPER			{ return OBJECT_FDW; }
		;

comment_text:
			Sconst								{ return $_[1]; }
			| NULL_P							{ return NULL; }
		;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *  SECURITY LABEL [FOR <provider>] ON <object> IS <label>
 *
 *  As with COMMENT ON, <object> can refer to various types of database
 *  objects (e.g. TABLE, COLUMN, etc.).
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

SecLabelStmt:
			SECURITY LABEL opt_provider ON security_label_type any_name
			IS security_label
				{
					SecLabelStmt *n = makeNode(SecLabelStmt);
					n->provider = $_[3];
					n->objtype = $_[5];
					n->objname = $_[6];
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->label = $_[8];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| SECURITY LABEL opt_provider ON AGGREGATE func_name aggr_args
			  IS security_label
				{
					SecLabelStmt *n = makeNode(SecLabelStmt);
					n->provider = $_[3];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_AGGREGATE;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					n->objargs = $_[7];
					n->label = $_[9];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| SECURITY LABEL opt_provider ON FUNCTION func_name func_args
			  IS security_label
				{
					SecLabelStmt *n = makeNode(SecLabelStmt);
					n->provider = $_[3];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_FUNCTION;
					n->objname = $_[6];
					n->objargs = extractArgTypes($_[7]);
					n->label = $_[9];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| SECURITY LABEL opt_provider ON LARGE_P OBJECT_P NumericOnly
			  IS security_label
				{
					SecLabelStmt *n = makeNode(SecLabelStmt);
					n->provider = $_[3];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_LARGEOBJECT;
					n->objname = list_make1($_[7]);
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->label = $_[9];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
			| SECURITY LABEL opt_provider ON opt_procedural LANGUAGE any_name
			  IS security_label
				{
					SecLabelStmt *n = makeNode(SecLabelStmt);
					n->provider = $_[3];
					n->objtype = OBJECT_LANGUAGE;
					n->objname = $_[7];
					n->objargs = NIL;
					n->label = $_[9];
					return (Node *) n;
				}
		;

opt_provider:	FOR ColId_or_Sconst	{ return $_[2]; }
				| /* empty */		{ return NULL; }
		;

security_label_type:
			COLUMN								{ return OBJECT_COLUMN; }
			| FOREIGN TABLE						{ return OBJECT_FOREIGN_TABLE; }
			| SCHEMA							{ return OBJECT_SCHEMA; }
			| SEQUENCE							{ return OBJECT_SEQUENCE; }
			| TABLE								{ return OBJECT_TABLE; }
			| DOMAIN_P							{ return OBJECT_TYPE; }
			| TYPE_P							{ return OBJECT_TYPE; }
			| VIEW								{ return OBJECT_VIEW; }
		;

security_label:	Sconst				{ return $_[1]; }
				| NULL_P			{ return NULL; }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERY:
 *			fetch/move
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

FetchStmt:	FETCH fetch_args
				{
					FetchStmt *n = (FetchStmt *) $_[2];
					n->ismove = FALSE;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| MOVE fetch_args
				{
					FetchStmt *n = (FetchStmt *) $_[2];
					n->ismove = TRUE;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

fetch_args:	cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[1];
					n->direction = FETCH_FORWARD;
					n->howMany = 1;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[2];
					n->direction = FETCH_FORWARD;
					n->howMany = 1;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| NEXT opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[3];
					n->direction = FETCH_FORWARD;
					n->howMany = 1;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| PRIOR opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[3];
					n->direction = FETCH_BACKWARD;
					n->howMany = 1;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| FIRST_P opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[3];
					n->direction = FETCH_ABSOLUTE;
					n->howMany = 1;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| LAST_P opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[3];
					n->direction = FETCH_ABSOLUTE;
					n->howMany = -1;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ABSOLUTE_P SignedIconst opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[4];
					n->direction = FETCH_ABSOLUTE;
					n->howMany = $_[2];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| RELATIVE_P SignedIconst opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[4];
					n->direction = FETCH_RELATIVE;
					n->howMany = $_[2];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| SignedIconst opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[3];
					n->direction = FETCH_FORWARD;
					n->howMany = $_[1];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| ALL opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[3];
					n->direction = FETCH_FORWARD;
					n->howMany = FETCH_ALL;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| FORWARD opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[3];
					n->direction = FETCH_FORWARD;
					n->howMany = 1;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| FORWARD SignedIconst opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[4];
					n->direction = FETCH_FORWARD;
					n->howMany = $_[2];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| FORWARD ALL opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[4];
					n->direction = FETCH_FORWARD;
					n->howMany = FETCH_ALL;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| BACKWARD opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[3];
					n->direction = FETCH_BACKWARD;
					n->howMany = 1;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| BACKWARD SignedIconst opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[4];
					n->direction = FETCH_BACKWARD;
					n->howMany = $_[2];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| BACKWARD ALL opt_from_in cursor_name
				{
					FetchStmt *n = makeNode(FetchStmt);
					n->portalname = $_[4];
					n->direction = FETCH_BACKWARD;
					n->howMany = FETCH_ALL;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

from_in:	FROM									{}
			| IN_P									{}
		;

opt_from_in:	from_in								{}
			| /* EMPTY */							{}
		;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * GRANT and REVOKE statements
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

GrantStmt:	GRANT privileges ON privilege_target TO grantee_list
			opt_grant_grant_option
				{
					GrantStmt *n = makeNode(GrantStmt);
					n->is_grant = true;
					n->privileges = $_[2];
					n->targtype = ($_[4])->targtype;
					n->objtype = ($_[4])->objtype;
					n->objects = ($_[4])->objs;
					n->grantees = $_[6];
					n->grant_option = $_[7];
					return (Node*)n;
				}
		;

RevokeStmt:
			REVOKE privileges ON privilege_target
			FROM grantee_list opt_drop_behavior
				{
					GrantStmt *n = makeNode(GrantStmt);
					n->is_grant = false;
					n->grant_option = false;
					n->privileges = $_[2];
					n->targtype = ($_[4])->targtype;
					n->objtype = ($_[4])->objtype;
					n->objects = ($_[4])->objs;
					n->grantees = $_[6];
					n->behavior = $_[7];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| REVOKE GRANT OPTION FOR privileges ON privilege_target
			FROM grantee_list opt_drop_behavior
				{
					GrantStmt *n = makeNode(GrantStmt);
					n->is_grant = false;
					n->grant_option = true;
					n->privileges = $_[5];
					n->targtype = ($_[7])->targtype;
					n->objtype = ($_[7])->objtype;
					n->objects = ($_[7])->objs;
					n->grantees = $_[9];
					n->behavior = $_[1]0;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;


/*
 * Privilege names are represented as strings; the validity of the privilege
 * names gets checked at execution.  This is a bit annoying but we have little
 * choice because of the syntactic conflict with lists of role names in
 * GRANT/REVOKE.  What's more, we have to call out in the "privilege"
 * production any reserved keywords that need to be usable as privilege names.
 */

/* either ALL [PRIVILEGES] or a list of individual privileges */
privileges: privilege_list
				{ return $_[1]; }
			| ALL
				{ return NIL; }
			| ALL PRIVILEGES
				{ return NIL; }
			| ALL '(' columnList ')'
				{
					AccessPriv *n = makeNode(AccessPriv);
					n->priv_name = NULL;
					n->cols = $_[3];
					return list_make1(n);
				}
			| ALL PRIVILEGES '(' columnList ')'
				{
					AccessPriv *n = makeNode(AccessPriv);
					n->priv_name = NULL;
					n->cols = $_[4];
					return list_make1(n);
				}
		;

privilege_list:	privilege							{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| privilege_list ',' privilege			{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

privilege:	SELECT opt_column_list
			{
				AccessPriv *n = makeNode(AccessPriv);
				n->priv_name = pstrdup($_[1]);
				n->cols = $_[2];
				return n;
			}
		| REFERENCES opt_column_list
			{
				AccessPriv *n = makeNode(AccessPriv);
				n->priv_name = pstrdup($_[1]);
				n->cols = $_[2];
				return n;
			}
		| CREATE opt_column_list
			{
				AccessPriv *n = makeNode(AccessPriv);
				n->priv_name = pstrdup($_[1]);
				n->cols = $_[2];
				return n;
			}
		| ColId opt_column_list
			{
				AccessPriv *n = makeNode(AccessPriv);
				n->priv_name = $_[1];
				n->cols = $_[2];
				return n;
			}
		;


/* Don't bother trying to fold the first two rules into one using
 * opt_table.  You're going to get conflicts.
 */
privilege_target:
			qualified_name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_RELATION;
					n->objs = $_[1];
					return n;
				}
			| TABLE qualified_name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_RELATION;
					n->objs = $_[2];
					return n;
				}
			| SEQUENCE qualified_name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_SEQUENCE;
					n->objs = $_[2];
					return n;
				}
			| FOREIGN DATA_P WRAPPER name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_FDW;
					n->objs = $_[4];
					return n;
				}
			| FOREIGN SERVER name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_FOREIGN_SERVER;
					n->objs = $_[3];
					return n;
				}
			| FUNCTION function_with_argtypes_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_FUNCTION;
					n->objs = $_[2];
					return n;
				}
			| DATABASE name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_DATABASE;
					n->objs = $_[2];
					return n;
				}
			| LANGUAGE name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_LANGUAGE;
					n->objs = $_[2];
					return n;
				}
			| LARGE_P OBJECT_P NumericOnly_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_LARGEOBJECT;
					n->objs = $_[3];
					return n;
				}
			| SCHEMA name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_NAMESPACE;
					n->objs = $_[2];
					return n;
				}
			| TABLESPACE name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_OBJECT;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_TABLESPACE;
					n->objs = $_[2];
					return n;
				}
			| ALL TABLES IN_P SCHEMA name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_ALL_IN_SCHEMA;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_RELATION;
					n->objs = $_[5];
					return n;
				}
			| ALL SEQUENCES IN_P SCHEMA name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_ALL_IN_SCHEMA;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_SEQUENCE;
					n->objs = $_[5];
					return n;
				}
			| ALL FUNCTIONS IN_P SCHEMA name_list
				{
					PrivTarget *n = (PrivTarget *) palloc(sizeof(PrivTarget));
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_ALL_IN_SCHEMA;
					n->objtype = ACL_OBJECT_FUNCTION;
					n->objs = $_[5];
					return n;
				}
		;


grantee_list:
			grantee									{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| grantee_list ',' grantee				{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

grantee:	RoleId
				{
					PrivGrantee *n = makeNode(PrivGrantee);
					/* This hack lets us avoid reserving PUBLIC as a keyword*/
					if (strcmp($_[1], "public") == 0)
						n->rolname = NULL;
					else
						n->rolname = $_[1];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| GROUP_P RoleId
				{
					PrivGrantee *n = makeNode(PrivGrantee);
					/* Treat GROUP PUBLIC as a synonym for PUBLIC */
					if (strcmp($_[2], "public") == 0)
						n->rolname = NULL;
					else
						n->rolname = $_[2];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;


opt_grant_grant_option:
			WITH GRANT OPTION { return TRUE; }
			| /*EMPTY*/ { return FALSE; }
		;

function_with_argtypes_list:
			function_with_argtypes					{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| function_with_argtypes_list ',' function_with_argtypes
													{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

function_with_argtypes:
			func_name func_args
				{
					FuncWithArgs *n = makeNode(FuncWithArgs);
					n->funcname = $_[1];
					n->funcargs = extractArgTypes($_[2]);
					return n;
				}
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * GRANT and REVOKE ROLE statements
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

GrantRoleStmt:
			GRANT privilege_list TO name_list opt_grant_admin_option opt_granted_by
				{
					GrantRoleStmt *n = makeNode(GrantRoleStmt);
					n->is_grant = true;
					n->granted_roles = $_[2];
					n->grantee_roles = $_[4];
					n->admin_opt = $_[5];
					n->grantor = $_[6];
					return (Node*)n;
				}
		;

RevokeRoleStmt:
			REVOKE privilege_list FROM name_list opt_granted_by opt_drop_behavior
				{
					GrantRoleStmt *n = makeNode(GrantRoleStmt);
					n->is_grant = false;
					n->admin_opt = false;
					n->granted_roles = $_[2];
					n->grantee_roles = $_[4];
					n->behavior = $_[6];
					return (Node*)n;
				}
			| REVOKE ADMIN OPTION FOR privilege_list FROM name_list opt_granted_by opt_drop_behavior
				{
					GrantRoleStmt *n = makeNode(GrantRoleStmt);
					n->is_grant = false;
					n->admin_opt = true;
					n->granted_roles = $_[5];
					n->grantee_roles = $_[7];
					n->behavior = $_[9];
					return (Node*)n;
				}
		;

opt_grant_admin_option: WITH ADMIN OPTION				{ return TRUE; }
			| /*EMPTY*/									{ return FALSE; }
		;

opt_granted_by: GRANTED BY RoleId						{ return $_[3]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/									{ return NULL; }
		;

/*****************************************************************************
 *
 * ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES statement
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

AlterDefaultPrivilegesStmt:
			ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES DefACLOptionList DefACLAction
				{
					AlterDefaultPrivilegesStmt *n = makeNode(AlterDefaultPrivilegesStmt);
					n->options = $_[4];
					n->action = (GrantStmt *) $_[5];
					return (Node*)n;
				}
		;

DefACLOptionList:
			DefACLOptionList DefACLOption			{ return lappend($_[1], $_[2]); }
			| /* EMPTY */							{ return NIL; }
		;

DefACLOption:
			IN_P SCHEMA name_list
				{
					return makeDefElem("schemas", (Node *)$_[3]);
				}
			| FOR ROLE name_list
				{
					return makeDefElem("roles", (Node *)$_[3]);
				}
			| FOR USER name_list
				{
					return makeDefElem("roles", (Node *)$_[3]);
				}
		;

/*
 * This should match GRANT/REVOKE, except that individual target objects
 * are not mentioned and we only allow a subset of object types.
 */
DefACLAction:
			GRANT privileges ON defacl_privilege_target TO grantee_list
			opt_grant_grant_option
				{
					GrantStmt *n = makeNode(GrantStmt);
					n->is_grant = true;
					n->privileges = $_[2];
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_DEFAULTS;
					n->objtype = $_[4];
					n->objects = NIL;
					n->grantees = $_[6];
					n->grant_option = $_[7];
					return (Node*)n;
				}
			| REVOKE privileges ON defacl_privilege_target
			FROM grantee_list opt_drop_behavior
				{
					GrantStmt *n = makeNode(GrantStmt);
					n->is_grant = false;
					n->grant_option = false;
					n->privileges = $_[2];
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_DEFAULTS;
					n->objtype = $_[4];
					n->objects = NIL;
					n->grantees = $_[6];
					n->behavior = $_[7];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| REVOKE GRANT OPTION FOR privileges ON defacl_privilege_target
			FROM grantee_list opt_drop_behavior
				{
					GrantStmt *n = makeNode(GrantStmt);
					n->is_grant = false;
					n->grant_option = true;
					n->privileges = $_[5];
					n->targtype = ACL_TARGET_DEFAULTS;
					n->objtype = $_[7];
					n->objects = NIL;
					n->grantees = $_[9];
					n->behavior = $_[1]0;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

defacl_privilege_target:
			TABLES			{ return ACL_OBJECT_RELATION; }
			| FUNCTIONS		{ return ACL_OBJECT_FUNCTION; }
			| SEQUENCES		{ return ACL_OBJECT_SEQUENCE; }
		;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERY: CREATE INDEX
 *
 * Note: we cannot put TABLESPACE clause after WHERE clause unless we are
 * willing to make TABLESPACE a fully reserved word.
 *****************************************************************************/

IndexStmt:	CREATE opt_unique INDEX opt_concurrently opt_index_name
			ON qualified_name access_method_clause '(' index_params ')'
			opt_reloptions OptTableSpace where_clause
				{
					IndexStmt *n = makeNode(IndexStmt);
					n->unique = $_[2];
					n->concurrent = $_[4];
					n->idxname = $_[5];
					n->relation = $_[7];
					n->accessMethod = $_[8];
					n->indexParams = $_[1]0;
					n->options = $_[12];
					n->tableSpace = $_[13];
					n->whereClause = $_[14];
					n->indexOid = InvalidOid;
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

opt_unique:
			UNIQUE									{ return TRUE; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return FALSE; }
		;

opt_concurrently:
			CONCURRENTLY							{ return TRUE; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return FALSE; }
		;

opt_index_name:
			index_name								{ return $_[1]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NULL; }
		;

access_method_clause:
			USING access_method						{ return $_[2]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return DEFAULT_INDEX_TYPE; }
		;

index_params:	index_elem							{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| index_params ',' index_elem			{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

/*
 * Index attributes can be either simple column references, or arbitrary
 * expressions in parens.  For backwards-compatibility reasons, we allow
 * an expression that's just a function call to be written without parens.
 */
index_elem:	ColId opt_collate opt_class opt_asc_desc opt_nulls_order
				{
					return makeNode(IndexElem);
					$$->name = $_[1];
					$$->expr = NULL;
					$$->indexcolname = NULL;
					$$->collation = $_[2];
					$$->opclass = $_[3];
					$$->ordering = $_[4];
					$$->nulls_ordering = $_[5];
				}
			| func_expr opt_collate opt_class opt_asc_desc opt_nulls_order
				{
					return makeNode(IndexElem);
					$$->name = NULL;
					$$->expr = $_[1];
					$$->indexcolname = NULL;
					$$->collation = $_[2];
					$$->opclass = $_[3];
					$$->ordering = $_[4];
					$$->nulls_ordering = $_[5];
				}
			| '(' a_expr ')' opt_collate opt_class opt_asc_desc opt_nulls_order
				{
					return makeNode(IndexElem);
					$$->name = NULL;
					$$->expr = $_[2];
					$$->indexcolname = NULL;
					$$->collation = $_[4];
					$$->opclass = $_[5];
					$$->ordering = $_[6];
					$$->nulls_ordering = $_[7];
				}
		;

opt_collate: COLLATE any_name						{ return $_[2]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NIL; }
		;

opt_class:	any_name								{ return $_[1]; }
			| USING any_name						{ return $_[2]; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return NIL; }
		;

opt_asc_desc: ASC							{ return SORTBY_ASC; }
			| DESC							{ return SORTBY_DESC; }
			| /*EMPTY*/						{ return SORTBY_DEFAULT; }
		;

opt_nulls_order: NULLS_FIRST				{ return SORTBY_NULLS_FIRST; }
			| NULLS_LAST					{ return SORTBY_NULLS_LAST; }
			| /*EMPTY*/						{ return SORTBY_NULLS_DEFAULT; }
		;


/*****************************************************************************
 *
 *		QUERY:
 *				create [or replace] function <fname>
 *						[(<type-1> { , <type-n>})]
 *						returns <type-r>
 *						as <filename or code in language as appropriate>
 *						language <lang> [with parameters]
 *
 *****************************************************************************/

CreateFunctionStmt:
			CREATE opt_or_replace FUNCTION func_name func_args_with_defaults
			RETURNS func_return createfunc_opt_list opt_definition
				{
					CreateFunctionStmt *n = makeNode(CreateFunctionStmt);
					n->replace = $_[2];
					n->funcname = $_[4];
					n->parameters = $_[5];
					n->returnType = $_[7];
					n->options = $_[8];
					n->withClause = $_[9];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE opt_or_replace FUNCTION func_name func_args_with_defaults
			  RETURNS TABLE '(' table_func_column_list ')' createfunc_opt_list opt_definition
				{
					CreateFunctionStmt *n = makeNode(CreateFunctionStmt);
					n->replace = $_[2];
					n->funcname = $_[4];
					n->parameters = mergeTableFuncParameters($_[5], $_[9]);
					n->returnType = TableFuncTypeName($_[9]);
					n->returnType->location = @7;
					n->options = $_[11];
					n->withClause = $_[12];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
			| CREATE opt_or_replace FUNCTION func_name func_args_with_defaults
			  createfunc_opt_list opt_definition
				{
					CreateFunctionStmt *n = makeNode(CreateFunctionStmt);
					n->replace = $_[2];
					n->funcname = $_[4];
					n->parameters = $_[5];
					n->returnType = NULL;
					n->options = $_[6];
					n->withClause = $_[7];
					return (Node *)n;
				}
		;

opt_or_replace:
			OR REPLACE								{ return TRUE; }
			| /*EMPTY*/								{ return FALSE; }
		;

func_args:	'(' func_args_list ')'					{ return $_[2]; }
			| '(' ')'								{ return NIL; }
		;

func_args_list:
			func_arg								{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
			| func_args_list ',' func_arg			{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

/*
 * func_args_with_defaults is separate because we only want to accept
 * defaults in CREATE FUNCTION, not in ALTER etc.
 */
func_args_with_defaults:
		'(' func_args_with_defaults_list ')'		{ return $_[2]; }
		| '(' ')'									{ return NIL; }
		;

func_args_with_defaults_list:
		func_arg_with_default						{ return list_make1($_[1]); }
		| func_args_with_defaults_list ',' func_arg_with_default
													{ return lappend($_[1], $_[3]); }
		;

/*
 * The style with arg_class first is SQL99 standard, but Oracle puts
 * param_name first; accept both since it's likely people will try both
 * anyway.  Don't bother trying to save productions by letting arg_class
 * have an empty alternative ... you'll get shift/reduce conflicts.
 *
 * We can catch over-specified arguments here if we want to,
 * but for now better to silently swallow typmod, etc.
 * - thomas 2000-03-22
 */
func_arg:
			arg_class param_name func_type
				{
					FunctionParameter *n = makeNode(FunctionParameter);
					n->name = $_[2];
					n->argType = $_[3];
					n->mode = $_[1];
					n->defexpr = NULL;
					return n;
				}
			| param_name arg_class func_type
				{
					FunctionParameter *n = makeNode(FunctionParameter);
					n->name = $_[1];
					n->argType = $_[3];
					n->mode = $_[2];
